## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task seeks the functional form of dP/dt given P and t, which is the right-hand side of a population dynamics ODE. The growth rate typically depends on population density through mechanisms like resource competition, Allee effects, or predation, and may include explicit time dependence for environmental variation.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, no density dependence)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Logistic with Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative at very low and very high densities)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism vs catabolism scaling)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (constant-effort harvesting)
- Logistic with constant yield harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (constant yield removal)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * (1 + c3) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Time-modulated logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (seasonal carrying capacity)
- Exponential with time-varying rate: dP_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) * P (time-dependent growth rate)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional-order density dependence)
- Logistic with immigration: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 (constant immigration term)
- Predation with type II response: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P / (1 + c2 * P) (growth with saturating predation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation → multiplicative factor (1 - P/K) or similar terms that change sign at carrying capacity
- Allee effect (mate-finding difficulty) → additional multiplicative factor (P - threshold) creating a lower critical population
- Gompertz-type deceleration → logarithmic dependence log(K/P) instead of linear (1 - P/K) for asymmetric growth curves
- Immigration/emigration → additive constant terms independent of P in the growth rate equation
- Seasonal/periodic environmental forcing → multiplicative or additive sinusoidal functions of time sin(c*t) or cos(c*t)
- Functional response in predation → rational terms P/(1 + c*P) or P^2/(1 + c*P^2) representing saturating consumption
- Metabolic scaling → different power-law exponents for gain vs loss terms (e.g., P^(2/3) - c*P) reflecting surface-to-volume ratios
- Dormancy/delay effects → terms involving exp(-c*t) representing transient initial dynamics before steady-state behavior
